-------------------------------- AXPY 500000, 1 devices ------------------------------
System has total 1 devices(1 GPU and 0 THSIM devices).
The number of each type of devices can be controlled by environment variables:
	OMP_NUM_THSIM_DEVICES for THSIM devices (default 0)
	OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting specific NVGPU devices (e.g., "0,2,3", i.e. ,separated list with no spaces)
	OMP_NUM_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting a number of NVIDIA GPU devices from dev 0 (default, total available, overwritten by OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES)
	To make a specific number of devices available, use OMP_NUM_ACTIVE_DEVICES (default, total number of system devices)

-------------------------------- AXPY 2000000, 8 devices ------------------------------
System has total 8 devices(8 GPU and 0 THSIM devices).
The number of each type of devices can be controlled by environment variables:
	OMP_NUM_THSIM_DEVICES for THSIM devices (default 0)
	OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting specific NVGPU devices (e.g., "0,2,3", i.e. ,separated list with no spaces)
	OMP_NUM_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting a number of NVIDIA GPU devices from dev 0 (default, total available, overwritten by OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES)
	To make a specific number of devices available, use OMP_NUM_ACTIVE_DEVICES (default, total number of system devices)
n = 2000000

-------------------------------- AXPY 4000000, 8 devices ------------------------------
System has total 8 devices(8 GPU and 0 THSIM devices).
The number of each type of devices can be controlled by environment variables:
	OMP_NUM_THSIM_DEVICES for THSIM devices (default 0)
	OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting specific NVGPU devices (e.g., "0,2,3", i.e. ,separated list with no spaces)
	OMP_NUM_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting a number of NVIDIA GPU devices from dev 0 (default, total available, overwritten by OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES)
	To make a specific number of devices available, use OMP_NUM_ACTIVE_DEVICES (default, total number of system devices)
n = 4000000

-------------------------------- AXPY 8000000, 8 devices ------------------------------
System has total 8 devices(8 GPU and 0 THSIM devices).
The number of each type of devices can be controlled by environment variables:
	OMP_NUM_THSIM_DEVICES for THSIM devices (default 0)
	OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting specific NVGPU devices (e.g., "0,2,3", i.e. ,separated list with no spaces)
	OMP_NUM_NVGPU_DEVICES for selecting a number of NVIDIA GPU devices from dev 0 (default, total available, overwritten by OMP_NVGPU_DEVICES)
	To make a specific number of devices available, use OMP_NUM_ACTIVE_DEVICES (default, total number of system devices)
n = 8000000
